Excellent habitat, sparse P-J (dominated by juniper ~3m high) on rocky slopes with sparse sagebrush understory. Saw 4 of 6 individuals and other two were heard singing typical fast song (about 1 phrase/sec, faster than typical PLVI song) 300-400m from other individuals.
